@13193  = ~History of Waterdeep—Age lV, The Return of the Lords: 

One day to the Courts of the Lord Magister came two people masked and robed as the Lords of Waterdeep of old. Where they came from no one knew, but they appeared in the Castle's Great Hall where the Courts were, and commanded the Lords Magister to leave the city forthwith. Laughing, the Lords Magister refused, whereupon the shorter of the masked intruders (the lady Shilam, apprentice to Ahghairon and his undeclared heir as first Lord of the City) blasted them with lightning and fire, and their very thrones were shattered and toppled. 

The taller of the two intruders (Baeron) then called for the heads of the noble houses to come to them, or leave the city forthwith and forever, if they cared not to come by nightfall. All in the Courts heard, and the news was cried in the streets. 

The surviving nobles came, reluctantly and with bodyguards, expecting such a summons to be a trap. Baeron spoke to them and the crowd of curious townsfolk that had also come, saying, "this must not happen again." If Waterdeep was to be safe once more, he told them, all must support what he and his fellow Lord now planned, as they had supported Ahghairon in the past. The two would choose others to be Lords as before, he said, and they would rule in secret, as before—save for himself. He removed his mask, and said, "I am Baeron. I would be Lord as Ahghairon was before. I would be safe in this my city again." And the folk of Waterdeep there agreed. Shilarn, still masked, commanded that the houses of the Two Lords Magister be Outcast. There was protest, and she raised her hands that had blasted the thrones, and it was still again. And the house of Gildeggh and of Zoar were outcast. 

Peace returned to the city, and Waterdhavians to their labors. To inhibit discovery of who the Lords were, Baeron selected certain men of character whom he knew well, and appointed them Magisters ("Black Robes," they were soon called, from their robes of office) under the Lords, to judge and apply the laws of Waterdeep in daily affairs. These Magisters he paid well, to raise them from temptation, and gave lodgings to those who feared for safety to dwell among the people. To so serve, he told the city, was a burden, not a proud misuse of authority, and if any wished to no longer serve, or were found wanting, they were not to be vilified, but accorded respect. And over the Magisters the Lords sat in their Court, to correct and overrule the judgments of the Magisters. Baeron told the people that none were to decry or belittle any judgments of Magisters that the Lord saw fit to alter or cast aside. If any thought ill of the offices or those who held them they could turn back to the rule of sword and whim, and perish as had those before them. Before the Lord's Court Baeron encouraged people to speak freely for the length of a short candle's burning, without fear of chastisement or reproach from the Lords for anything said, as long as they spoke openly and answered questions or opposing views put to them by any there. Thus, he held, just grievances of folk would be heard, no matter how small the matter or lowly the speaker. And so it was. Slow to take hold, until people knew it for careful justice, but enduring beyond Baeron's time, and beyond Shilarn's time, and beyond the time of their daughter Lhestyn "The Masked Lady," who wed Zelphar Arunsun of Neverwinter, and was mother to Khelben "Blackstaff' Arunsun, a Lord of Waterdeep today, who knows the secrets of long years as Ahghairon did. And as the years have passed, Waterdeep has grown in size and variety, flourishing with good trade under the tolerance and protection of strong defenders and good government. The years passed not without troubles, varying from the Godswar (when Waterdeep played host to gods dying and ascending) to such occurrences as a green dragon assailing the Field of Triumph (part of a plot by the Knights of the Shield to overthrow the Lords' Rule), but the city and her peoples survived and prevailed against all strife. The Lords' Alliance provides continued safety for all the settlements of the northern Sword Coast and those inland, with Waterdeep as the heart of the alliance. Though it can be matched in size or commerce, there is no city the realms over that compares to the sheer variety of life and experiences found in fair Waterdeep, Crown of the North. 《深水城歷史，第四時期，領主的歸回：

有一天，行政官法庭前來了兩個人，他們蒙著面具，穿著像是深水城舊領主的衣飾。沒有人知道他們從哪兒來，他們出現在城堡的大廳中，也就是法庭所在，並命令行政官立刻離開這座城。行政官們大笑著拒絕了，蒙面闖入者中比較矮的那位（西蓮小姐，艾哈倫未公開的繼承人，這座城的第一位領主）立刻用雷和火轟向他們，他們的王座隨即碎裂倒下。

兩名闖入者中較高的那位（拜倫）命令貴族的領袖集合，不然就馬上離開這座城，永遠不准再回來。法庭內的其他人都聽到這件事，消息馬上在大接小巷傳了開來。

貴族們帶著保鏢不情願地到來，期望著這次召喚只是個玩笑。拜倫對著他們以及好奇尾隨而來的群眾說：「這絕不會再發生了。」如果希望深水城能再度恢復和平，他表示，所有人必須支持他和他的領主夥伴，就如同支持舊時的艾哈倫一般。他們兩個將會跟從前一樣選出其他的領主，也會像從前一樣秘密治理，以確認他們的安全。他摘下面具，說：「我是拜倫。我將成為像艾哈倫一樣的領主。我要讓這座城市在我的治理下再歸和平。」深水城的人民隨即同意。西蓮仍然戴著面具，並下令放逐兩位執政官的家族。有人表示抗議，但她舉起她轟掉王座的的手之後，反對者就再度沉默。於是，吉德吉和洛耳兩族就被流放了。

和平再度降臨到這座城市，及其港口與人民身上。為了讓人不知道誰是領主，拜倫選了幾個熟悉的人，指派他們為領主手下的行政官（他們隨即被稱為「黑袍」，因為他們制服是黑色的）來處理及仲裁深水城的一般事務。他給予這些行政官豐富的報酬，並建立官邸供這些無法住在人群中的人居住。他告訴市民，這些公僕差事是件負擔，不可拿來作為權威的象徵；如果有人不想再服務，或是處事不能盡如人意，他們也不該被指責。而且在行政官之上，還有領主們坐鎮在法庭中，修正或駁回行政官的誤判。如果任何人對領主及行政官有非份之想，或是想回頭使用武力至上的規則，他們就會被毀滅。拜倫鼓勵人們，在領主法庭前可以暢所欲言，不用畏懼懲罰，不用怕丟臉，批評領主也沒關係，他們會公開回答任何人質疑的問題，也容許相反的意見。任何委屈也都可以來申訴，無論事情多小、申訴者身份有多低微都沒關係。剛開始領主法庭前還門可羅雀，但人民逐漸瞭解到它關心公理的用意。深水城歷經了拜倫的時代、西蓮的時代、以及他們女兒「蒙面淑女」羅絲汀的時代。羅絲汀與絕冬城來的賽爾法·奧羅桑結婚，生下了凱爾本·「黑杖」·奧羅桑。他繼任為現在的領主，知道與遠古的艾哈倫同樣多的秘密。這麼多年來，深水城持續成長擴大，在強大
而善良的政府保護之下，貿易十分興盛。但這些年來也不完全和平，就在諸神之戰時（深水城是許多神興起及長眠之地），一隻綠龍襲擊了勝利荒地（鋼盾騎士團推翻領主統治的陰謀之一），但這座城和他的人民存活下來，並與各種紛亂對抗。領主聯盟持續提供對劍灣北部，以及周圍群島居民的安全保護，深水城就是這個聯盟的中心。雖然它的城市大小和貿易量都有限，但世界上還沒有哪座城敢跟深水城，這座北地之冠相抗衡。》~

@14254  = ~Fire Seeds
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 6
Sphere: Elemental
Range: 0
Duration: 3 turns
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: 1/2

Casting the Fire Seed spell creates 4 fire seeds that will appear in the caster's inventory. The seeds will remain in existence for 3 turns after the spell is cast. If they are thrown at an enemy, a fireball will ensue, causing 2d8 points of damage to all within a 7-ft. radius unless they make a Saving Throw vs. Spell for half damage.《火種術（咒法/召喚系）
等級：6
領域：元素系
有效距離：特殊
持續時間：3回合
施法時間：1輪
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：1/2傷害

此法術可以在牧師的物品欄中製造出4顆火焰種子，它們可以維持3回合的時間。在這段期間之內，可以將它們射出投向敵人，爆炸為一團可造成2-16點傷害的火球。火術作用範圍內的所有生物都會受到傷害，如果通過對法術的豁免檢定則只會受到一半的傷害。》~

@15180  = ~Conjure Earth Elemental《召喚土元素》~
@15181  = ~Conjure Earth Elemental 
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 7
Sphere: Elemental (Earth), Summoning
Range: Visual range of the caster
Duration: 1 turn/level
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

Upon casting a Conjure Earth Elemental spell, the caster opens a special gate to the Elemental Plane of Earth, and an earth elemental is summoned in the vicinity of the caster. There is a 60% chance that a 12-Hit-Dice elemental appears, a 35% chance that a 16-Hit-Dice elemental appears, and a 5% chance that a 24-Hit-Dice elemental appears. All of the commands given to the elemental are done telepathically, so there is no time lost due to miscommunication, and it is not necessary to know the language of the summoned creature. Unlike Mages, priests do not have to engage in a battle of the minds to control their summoned elemental.《召喚土元素（咒法/召喚系）
等級：7
領域：元素，召喚
有效距離：施法者視線所及
持續時間：1回合/每等級
施法時間：1輪
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

施展召喚土元素法術，牧師可開啟一道通往土元素界的特殊傳送門，召喚出一名土元素到施法者的身邊。有60%的機會可召喚出12顆生命骰數的土元素，35%的機會召出16顆生命骰數的土元素，5%的機會召出24顆生命骰數的土元素。所有的命令都以精神感應的方式進行，不會浪費任何的時間或是有誤解的產生，也不需要瞭解被召喚生物的語言。與法師不同的是，牧師並不需要和召喚出的元素進行心靈意志的對抗，所召喚出來的元素會聽從施法者的所有命令，直到被殺死或是法術時效結束為止。》~

@15212  = ~Conjure Fire Elemental
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 6
Sphere: Elemental (Fire), Summoning
Range: Visual range of the caster
Duration: 1 turn/level
Casting Time: 9
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

Upon casting a Conjure Fire Elemental spell, the caster opens a special gate to the Elemental Plane of Fire, and a fire elemental is summoned in the vicinity of the caster. There is a 60% chance that a 12-Hit-Dice elemental appears; a 35% chance that a 16-Hit-Dice elemental appears; and a 5% chance that a 24-Hit-Dice elemental appears. The elemental will do the bidding of the caster until it is slain or the duration of the spell runs out. All the commands given to the elemental are done telepathically, so there is no time lost due to miscommunication and no need to know the language of the summoned creature. Unlike Mages, priests do not have to engage in a battle of the minds to control their elemental.《召喚火元素（咒法/召喚系）
等級：6
領域：元素，召喚
有效距離：施法者視線所及
持續時間：1回合/每等級
施法時間：1輪
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

@15988  = ~Carrion Crawler
The carrion crawler is a scavenger of subterranean areas, feeding primarily upon carrion. However, when such food becomes scarce or when it is threatened, it will attack and kill living creatures.

The carrion crawler looks like a cross between a giant green cutworm and a cephalopod. Like so many other hybrid monsters, the carrion crawler may well be the result of genetic experimentation by a mad, evil wizard. 

The monster's head is covered with a tough hide, but the body is not well protected. The monster is accompanied by a rank, fetid odor which often gives warning of its approach.《食腐蟲
食腐蟲是地底的食腐生物，他們的主要食物是腐屍。但是當他們的主食來源不足時，他們也會攻擊活生生的倒霉傢伙。
食腐蟲看起來像是巨大的蚯蚓和血蛭的混種。就如同其他可怕的怪物一樣，食腐蟲也許是某個瘋狂巫師的基因實驗品。
食腐蟲的頭部覆蓋有非常堅硬的外殼，但是身體就比較柔軟。食腐蟲常常帶有一股惡臭的味道，可讓人提前警覺它的到來。
》~

@15990  = ~Ettercap
Ettercaps are ugly bipedal creatures that get along very well with all types of giant spiders. These creatures of low intelligence are exceedingly cruel, very cunning, and are skilled in setting traps—very deadly traps—much like the spiders that often live around them.

Ettercaps stand around six feet tall, even with their stooping gait and hunched shoulders. The creatures have short, spindly legs, long arms that reach nearly to their ankles, and large pot-bellies. The hands of ettercaps have a thumb and three long fingers that end in razor sharp claws. Their bodies are covered by tufts of thick, wiry, black hair, and their skin is dark and thick. Ettercaps' heads are almost equine in shape, but they have large reptilian eyes, usually blood-red in color, and large fangs, one protruding downward from each side of the mouth. The mouth itself is large and lined with very sharp teeth.

Ettercaps do not have a formal language. They express themselves through a combination of high-pitched chittering noises, shrieks and violent actions.《伊特怪
伊特怪是一種外型醜陋的雙足步行生物，它們和各種巨大蜘蛛之間的關係十分要好。這些生物雖然智商很低，但是卻十分殘酷狡詐，並且擅於設計陷阱（非常致命的陷阱），這和它們周圍的蜘蛛可說是十分相像。
雖然伊特怪突腹、駝背，但它們站立起來仍約有六尺高。這種生物具有類似蜘蛛的短腿，以及幾乎長到腳踝的細瘦雙臂，還有胖而突出的肚子。伊特怪的手有三根指頭和一根拇指，每根指頭的尾端都是鋒利的爪子。它們的身體覆蓋了一層粗黑捲曲的毛髮，皮膚則是深黑色。伊特怪擁有一顆非常大的頭，以及一對巨大血紅的爬蟲類雙眼，巨大的獠牙從嘴角向外伸出。它們的血盆大口中長有非常銳利的牙齒。伊特怪沒有正式的語言，他們利用獠牙的摩擦和各式各樣的方法發出尖銳刺耳的聲音進行溝通。
》~
@15991  = ~Ghoul
Ghouls are undead creatures, once human, who now feed on the flesh of corpses. Although the change from human to ghoul has deranged and destroyed their minds, ghouls have a terrible cunning which enables them to hunt their prey most effectively.

Ghouls are vaguely recognizable as once having been human, but have become horribly disfigured by their change to ghouls. The tongue becomes long and tough for licking marrow from cracked bones, the teeth become sharp and elongated, and the nails grow strong and sharp like claws.《食屍鬼
食屍鬼是不死生物，它們曾經是活生生的人類，現在卻變成以屍體為食的無意識生物。雖然由人類變成食屍鬼的過程徹底摧毀了它們的思想，但是食屍鬼強烈的獵捕本能，使它們成為非常有效的獵食者。
從食屍鬼的外型還勉強可以看得出來它們曾經是人類，但是身上許多地方卻都嚴重扭曲變形。它們的舌頭變成又長又硬，專門用來舔食骨頭中的骨髓，而牙齒則變得又尖又利，指甲則變得堅硬鋒利。
》~

@15994  = ~Gibberling 
They come screaming, jabbering, and howling out of the night. Dozens, maybe hundreds, of hunchbacked, naked humanoids swarm unceasingly forward. They have no thought of safety, subtlety, or strategy, leaving others with no hope of stopping their mass assault. Then, having come and killed, the gibberlings move on, seemingly randomly, back into the night.

The first impression of gibberlings is of a writhing mass of fur and flesh in the distant moonlit darkness. The pandemonium is actually a mass of pale, hunchbacked humanoids, with pointed canine ears and black manes surrounding their hideous, grinning faces. Their black eyes shine with a maniacal gleam.《狂猿
這些怪物在深夜尖嘯狂吼，四處奔跑。數十至數百個駝背的赤裸類人生物蜂擁而出，它們似乎不知道什麼是安全或戰術，這常讓其他生物對它們的侵犯感到束手無策。就在它們大開殺戒之後，這些狂猿們又漫無目的地消失在夜空之中。
狂猿給人的第一印象，就像是月光底下一團扭曲的毛髮和血肉的混合體。實際上，這些像惡魔的生物具有雜亂的黑色毛髮和尖耳朵，臉龐四周有著黑色鬃毛，時常帶著邪異的微笑。它們的黑色眼睛閃著瘋狂的光芒。
》~
@15995  = ~Gnoll
Gnolls are large, evil, hyena-like humanoids that roam about in loosely organized bands.

While the body of a gnoll is shaped like that of a large human, the details are those of a hyena. They stand erect on two legs and have hands that can manipulate as well as those of any human. They have greenish gray skin, darker near the muzzle, with a short reddish gray to dull yellow mane.《豺狼人
豺狼人是巨大、邪惡，如同土狼一般的人型生物，它們成群結隊地活動，但是群組織十分鬆散。
雖然豺狼人的身體看起來像是高大的人類，但是仔細觀察可以看得出它擁有土狼的遺傳特徵。它們用兩腳直立，雙手可以和正常人類一樣使用各種工具。它們的皮膚是黑綠色，靠近鼻子的地方是一團黑，黃色的毛髮中則帶著些許灰紅色。
》~
@15996  = ~Hobgoblin
Hobgoblins are a fierce humanoid race that wage perpetual war with the other humanoid races. They are intelligent, organized, and aggressive. 

The typical hobgoblin is a burly humanoid standing at least six feet tall. Their hairy hides range from dark reddish-brown to dark gray. Their faces show dark red or red-orange skin. Large males have blue or red noses. Hobgoblin eyes are either yellowish or dark brown while their teeth are yellow. Their garments tend to be brightly colored, often bold, blood red. Any leather is always tinted black. Hobgoblin weaponry is kept polished and repaired.

Hobgoblins have their own language and often speak with orcs, goblins, and carnivorous apes.《大地精
大地精是性格暴烈的種族，時常和其他類人征戰，它們擁有智慧、群組織和強烈的侵略性。
典型的大地精至少有六尺高，相當壯碩。它們多毛的外皮色澤則是從暗紅棕色到黑灰色，臉孔是紅色或橘紅色。大地精的眼珠不是棕色就是黃色，而它們的牙齒通常都是黃色。它們的服裝通常色澤鮮艷，大部分都是鮮紅或血紅色，皮革部分則都染成黑色。大地精常常進行武器保養和修復工作。
》~
@15997  = ~Kobold 
Kobolds are a cowardly, sadistic race of short humanoids that vigorously contest the human and demihuman races for living space and food. They especially dislike gnomes and attack them on sight.

Barely clearing three feet in height, kobolds have scaly hides that range from dark, rusty brown to a rusty black. They smell of damp dogs and stagnant water. Their eyes glow like a pair of bright red sparks, and they have two small horns ranging from tan to white. Because of the kobold fondness for wearing raggedy garb of red and orange, their non-prehensile rat-like tails, and their language (which sounds like small dogs yapping), these fell creatures are often not taken seriously. This is often a fatal mistake, for what they lack in size and strength they make up in ferocity and tenacity.《狗頭人
狗頭人是懦弱膽小的矮小人型生物，它們和人類或其他類人生物共同競爭生活資源和空間。它們特別討厭侏儒，只要一看到他們就會發動攻擊。
一般的狗頭人幾近三尺高，他們皮膚的色澤從紅棕色到黑灰色，眼睛發著紅光，並且擁有兩根小角。由於狗頭人特別喜歡穿著破爛的橘紅或是紅色衣物，再加上他們無毛的老鼠尾巴，以及他們的語言聽起來像是小狗汪汪叫，所以許多人會小看這些污穢的生物。這是個很要命的錯誤，因為他們在體型和力量上的弱點，都可以由他們的火爆和頑強個性所彌補。
》~
@15998  = ~Ogre
Ogres are big, ugly, greedy humanoids that live by ambushes, raids, and theft. Ill-tempered and nasty, these monsters are often found serving as mercenaries in the ranks of orc tribes, evil clerics, or gnolls. They mingle freely with giants and trolls.

Adult ogres stand nine to ten feet tall and weigh 300 to 350 pounds. Their skin colors range from a dead yellow to a dull black-brown, and (rarely) a sickly violet. Their warty bumps are often of a different color—or at least darker than their hides. Their eyes are purple with white pupils. Teeth and talons are orange or black. Ogres have long, greasy hair of blackish blue to dull dark green. Their odor is repellent, reminiscent of curdled milk. Dressing in poorly cured furs and animal hides, they care for their weapons and armor only reasonably well.

It is common for ogres to speak orc, troll, stone giant, and gnoll, as well as their own guttural language. A typical ogre's life span is 90 years.《食人魔
食人魔是以偷襲、劫掠和偷盜為生的巨大醜惡貪婪類人生物。他們不但手段卑劣，而且脾氣也很不好，通常居於半獸人部落、邪惡牧師手下，或是和豺狼人一起擔任傭兵。他們和巨人或是巨魔常常一起出沒。成年的食人魔身高大約九到十尺，體重大約三百到三百五十磅。他們皮膚的顏色從暗黃色到呆板的黑棕色，在極為少數的狀況下，還會有病態的紫色。他們身上大大小小的腫瘤通常和皮膚的顏色不同，最少也會比較深一些。他們的眼珠是紫色的，瞳孔則是白色。食人魔的頭髮是黑藍色或暗綠色，他們的臭味又濃又重，聞起來就像壞掉的牛奶一樣。他們穿著由獸皮縫製的簡陋服裝，對武器不太保養。一般食人魔通常都會說半獸人、豺狼人、巨魔、石巨人的語言。一名普通的的食人魔擁有九十年以上的壽命。
》~
@15999  = ~Skeleton
All skeletons are magically animated undead monsters, created as guardians or warriors by powerful evil wizards and priests.

Skeletons appear to have no ligaments or musculature which would allow movement. Instead, the bones are magically joined together during the casting of an Animate Dead spell. Skeletons have no eyes or internal organs.

Skeletons can be made from the bones of humans and demihumans, animals of human size or smaller, or giant humanoids like bugbears and giants.《骷髏
所有骷髏都是利用魔法操縱的不死怪物，它們是被邪惡而且法力強大的巫師或牧師所創造出來的戰士或守衛。
骷髏看起來沒有任何肌肉或是肌腱可以幫助它們移動。由此可知，這些骨頭是利用操縱死屍的法術而結合在一起。骷髏沒有眼睛，也沒有任何的體內器官。
骷髏的骨骼可以是人類、半人類、接近人類體型的動物，或巨大的人型生物。
》~
@16000  = ~Giant Spider
Spiders are aggressive predators, dwelling both above and below ground. Most are poisonous and bite prey before devouring them because unconscious victims are easier to carry to a lair.

Spiders have eight legs and eight eyes. They usually fit into two categories: web-spinners, which have bulbous abdomens and thin, sleek legs; and hunting spiders, which have smaller bodies, larger heads and fangs, and hairy bodies and legs.

Most giant spiders are simply much bigger versions of the web-spinning large spiders.《巨蜘蛛
蜘蛛是具有強烈侵略性的獵食者，它們居住在地表。大多數的巨蜘蛛擁有強烈的毒性，把獵物吞吃下肚之前會先咬獵物一口，因為昏迷的獵物能夠比較方便搬回巢穴。
蜘蛛擁有八隻腳和八對眼睛。它們有兩種類型：一種是織網者，這類的蜘蛛擁有圓鼓鼓的小腹和細長的腿；另一種則是獵食者，它們體型比較小，頭卻比較大，牙齒也比較粗，身體和腿上也擁有比較多黑毛。
大多數的巨蜘蛛只是一般織網蜘蛛的放大版。如果被巨蜘蛛咬了一口，而受害者對毒物的豁免檢定又失敗的話，便會立刻死亡。》~

@16165  = ~Monster Summoning IV
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 6
Range: 120 ft.
Duration: 5 rounds + 1 round/level
Casting Time: 6
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

This spell is much like the 3rd-level monster summoning I spell, except that this spell summons 6-HD monsters. There is a 60% chance of receiving one monster and a 40% chance of receiving two monsters. These monster(s) appear within spell range and attack the caster's opponents until the spell duration expires or until they are slain. 《四級召喚怪物術（咒法/召喚系）
等級：6
有效距離：40碼
持續時間：5輪+1輪/每等級
施法時間：6
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

此法術的作用類似於第三級的一級召喚怪物術，所不同者在於此法術可召喚出生命骰數為6的怪物。有60%的機率只召喚出一隻怪物，40%的機率召喚出兩隻怪物。所召喚的怪物將會出現在有效距離內的指定地點，開始攻擊施法者的敵人，直到法術效力結束或是被殺死為止。》~

@16170  = ~Monster Summoning V
(Conjuration/Summoning)

Level: 7
Range: 120 ft.
Duration: 6 rounds + 1 round/level
Casting Time: 6
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

Within one round of casting this spell, the wizard magically conjures 1d4 5-HD monsters. These monster(s) appear within spell range and attack the caster's opponents until the spell duration expires or until they are slain. 《五級召喚怪物術（咒法/召喚系）

有效距離：40碼
持續時間：6輪+1輪/每等級
施法時間：6
影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：無

這個法術施展後，法師將會呼喚出一到四個五級的怪物。怪物們會出現在法術的有效距離內，並且攻擊施法者的敵人，一直持續到法術效力結束或是怪物被殺為止。》~

_
If you have a Mage, Cleric, or Druid in your party, your character must memorize spells using the Rest button on the Mage Book or Priest Scroll pages. To get to these pages, right-click on your character portrait and then select the Book or Scroll icon that appears on the left.
《
_
如果你的隊伍裡有法師、牧師或德魯伊，你可以在法師的魔法書或牧師卷軸的畫面中按「休息」按鈕來記憶法術。若想要開啟這些畫面，只須在人物畫像上按鼠標右鍵，再選擇左邊的書或卷軸圖像即可。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16216  = ~
_
You can look at your Inventory page by right-clicking on your character portrait.
《
_
若想要查看人物的物品欄，只須直接在他的畫像上按鼠標右鍵即可。但在察看物品欄時，遊戲會取消暫停，所以戰鬥中務必小心。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16217  = ~
_
Equip items by placing them in the appropriate slots around your character on the Inventory page. Once equipped, you can pick the weapon you wish to use by left-clicking on the Quick Weapon slot at the bottom of the main gameplay screen. A green box will appear around the weapon that is in your character's hands; an orange box indicates combat mode.
《
_
如果你要裝備物品，只須把它們放在物品欄畫面中人物圖四周的適當欄位即可。一旦裝備好，你就可以在主遊戲畫面下方的立即可用武器欄中，按鼠標左鍵選擇使用。綠色格子表示你的人物目前使用的武器，橘色格子則表示處於戰鬥狀態。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16218  = ~
_
You can pause the game at any time by hitting the space bar or left-clicking on the clock face. Unpausing occurs the same way. Pausing is most useful during combat where it gives you the time to carefully orchestrate your party's attack.
《
_
如果你想要暫停遊戲，你可以隨時按空白鍵，或是在時鐘的圖像上按鼠標左鍵。取消暫停也是一樣的按法。但是在你察看物品欄時，也會自動取消暫停。暫停功能在戰鬥時很有用，它可以讓你仔細地編排隊伍的戰鬥編製。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16219  = ~
_
Buy items by talking to the keeper of a store or inn. You can also rest your party by renting a room, try to hear a few rumors over a mug of ale, or attempt a little shoplifting. In the Buy/Sell screen, items that the currently selected character cannot use (due to class limitations or weapon proficiencies) will be tinted red, though others in your party may have a use for them. 
《
_
如果要買東西，你可以和商店或旅館的老闆交談。你也可以租房間休息、買酒聽閒談，或試著在店裡順手牽羊。在買賣畫面中，該人物因故不能使用的物品（例如因為職業限制或武器特長的限制）會以紅色顯示，但也許其他隊員可以使用。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16220  = ~
_
While in temples, talk to the priests as you would an innkeeper. They offer an array of useful services, and you will often be able to heal your party, purchase specialty items, or identify treasures acquired during your travels.
《
_
在神殿中，你可以跟牧師交談，這就像在旅店裡跟旅店老闆講話一樣。他們會提供一些有用的服務。你可以幫你的隊員治療、買賣特殊物品，或鑒識冒險中得到的寶物。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16221  = ~
_
Thieves access their skills using the icons along the bottom of their screen. "Thieving" includes Open Locks, Pick Pockets, and Remove Trap, when used in conjunction with the appropriate targets (chests, people, and traps, respectively). "Find Traps" examines a general area and outlines found traps in red. "Stealth" uses Move Silently and Hide in Shadows to render a Thief effectively invisible until their next attack. That attack is automatically a backstab, increasing the damage of a successful hit dramatically.
《
_
盜賊可以用畫面下方的圖像來使用特殊技能。盜賊技能包含扒竊、開鎖和移除陷阱，該人物會因目標物不同（人、陷阱、箱子或門）而自動判斷該作什麼。「找尋陷阱」會檢查一整塊區域，並將陷阱標上紅色。「潛行」可讓該人物藏身黑暗不被看見，直到下次展開攻擊為止。潛行時的攻擊自動設為「背刺」，如果背刺成功，傷害力會大幅增加。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16222  = ~
_
Clerics and Paladins have the ability to Turn Undead. Activating this icon will cause many undead creatures to flee or even be destroyed. When in this mode, the character can move wherever they wish. Any other action, such as attacking or casting a spell, will deactivate the ability. 
《
_
牧師和聖武士都可以超度不死生物。若超度成功，可以使許多不死生物逃跑，或甚至將其摧毀。在超度時，你的人物可以隨意走動。但是其他行動，例如攻擊或施法，則會中斷超度的過程。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16223  = ~
_
Bards can inspire their comrades in combat by use of the Bard Song. They are able to move when singing, but any other action will end the song. While they may be rogues, Bards primarily concern themselves with people. Because of this, they can pick pockets but lack the other thieving skills. 
《
_
吟遊詩人可以使用吟唱歌曲的技能來鼓舞夥伴。他們可以邊唱歌邊移動，不過一旦作出別的動作就不能吟唱。雖然吟遊詩人有時像是盜賊，但是他們喜歡與人親近。因此他們只會扒竊，卻不具備盜賊的其他技能。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16224  = ~
_
Open doors by left-clicking on the doorway. The mouse pointer will change into a door icon when in the right position and the door will be outlined in blue. Your party can then enter the building if you left-click on the area just inside the door. 
《
_
對著門口按鼠標左鍵便可開門。當鼠標游標移到正確位置時，會變成門的圖像，門的邊框會變成藍色。對著門按鼠標左鍵，你的隊伍就可以進入該棟建築物。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16225  = ~
_
Direct your selected character to climb stairs by moving the pointer to the top of a stairway and left-clicking. The graphic will change to a stair icon when in the right spot.
《
_
若想要讓人物上下樓梯，只須把鼠標游標移到樓梯上，然後按鼠標左鍵。當鼠標游標移到正確位置時，會變成樓梯圖案。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16226  = ~
_
Hostile creatures have red circles around their feet. Left-clicking within the circle will direct your character to attack. You can switch weapons using the Quick Weapon icons. The weapon outlined in green is the current weapon. Attack with fists only (empty Quick Slot) if you only wish to knock your opponent unconscious. If you have a character with magical abilities, try casting a spell using their Spell icons. 
《
_
有敵意的生物腳下會有紅色的圓圈。對圓圈按鼠標左鍵，你的人物就會展開攻擊。你可以運用立即可用武器欄更換武器。目前使用的武器是以綠框表示。若是只想把對方打昏，可以選擇空手戰鬥（選擇空白欄位）。如果你的人物會使用法術，可以選用法術圖像來施法。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16227  = ~
_
If you are having trouble coordinating your attacks, try pressing the space bar to pause the game. While paused, issue your commands. When you unpause the game, your characters will obey the orders you have given them.
《
_
如果你對攻擊調度感到困難，可以試著按下空白鍵暫停遊戲。你可以在暫停時對人物下指令，之後取消暫停，他們就會依你下的指令行動。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16228  = ~
_
Interaction defaults to Talk for neutral targets and Attack for hostile targets. To talk to a neutral character (neutrals are identified by blue circles), left-click on one of them. Don't forget to select one of your party members to do the talking. If you would like to talk to a hostile character, select the Talk icon and then left-click on the character. If you would like to attack a neutral, select a weapon icon and then left-click on the target.
《
_
對中立人物按下鼠標的預設動作是「交談」，對有敵意目標的預設動作則是「攻擊」。想要跟中立人物交談（中立人物腳下會有藍色的圓圈），只須直接對著他們按鼠標左鍵。不要忘了先選擇隊伍中的某一個人物去和他交談。如果你想要和有敵意的目標交談，就先選擇交談圖像，再對目標人物按鼠標左鍵。如果你想要攻擊中立人物，就要先選擇武器的圖像，再對該人物按鼠標左鍵。

》~ [TEXTPOP]
@16229  = ~
_
Wizards, Clerics, Druids, and Bards can all cast spells. Select their Cast Spell button, choose a spell, and left-click on your target. You can also configure Quick Spells by right-clicking on a Quick Spell slot. This summons a list of memorized spells to choose. If no spells are listed, the character either does not have any spells memorized or cannot cast until higher levels. To cast the Quick Spell, left-click on the appropriate Quick Spell slot and then select your target.
《
_
法師、牧師、德魯伊和吟遊詩人都可以施法。欲施法時，須選擇他們的施法圖像（畫面左方），再選定法術，然後對著目標按鼠標左鍵。你也可以按鼠標右鍵來設定立即可施法術欄位（畫面下方）。設定時會列出一張該人物已記憶的法術清單。如果清單上沒有任何法術，表示該人物可能尚未記憶法術或等級不夠。若想快速施法，便選擇想要用的立即可施法術欄，按鼠標左鍵，然後再選擇目標。

Wands are powered by charges, each use costing one or more charges (depending on the item). When a wand runs out of charges, it is consumed and destroyed.

STATISTICS:

Weight: 1《法杖是四分之一呎長的棍子。它的材質包括象牙、骨頭和木材，尖端通常鑲有鐵器、水晶或石球之類的物品。法杖很脆弱，一不小心就會折斷或敲碎。因此它們多被儲存在箱子裡。

法杖都帶有魔法，但是有使用次數的限制（依物品而定），每次使用都會損耗能量。當能量用完後，法杖就會損毀。

@16273  = ~Splint mail is a variant of banded mail in which the metal strips are applied vertically to the backing of chain, leather, or cloth rather than horizontally as in banded mail. Since the body does not swivel in mid-torso as much as it flexes back to front, splint mail is more restrictive in battle. 

STATISTICS:

Armor Class: 3 (2 vs. piercing and missile, 1 vs. crushing)
Requires:
 8 Strength

Weight: 20《直行鏈甲是鎖子甲的一種變體。它的鎖鏈和鋼環是以垂直的方式加在衣物、皮革或鐵鏈之後，與其他盔甲慣用的水平方向不同。因為人類的身體其實比較常做垂直方向的運動，所以它在戰鬥時所受到的局限較大。

資料資料：
防禦等級：3

@16274  = ~Bracers are thick bands of metal or leather that are strapped, belted, or tied to a character's forearm. Generally, the magic that is instilled in bracers is good only during combat, since most bracers help protect the wearer from injury or improve their chances to strike an opponent. Exceptions do exist, though such specialized items are rare at best.
